Hi

I used WineLib with Mono 0.25 on Red Hat 9

I downloaded the latest RPM version of WINE from their sourceforge
projectpage (in my case I took the one for RH9 with Athlon CPU) and
installed it

Then I downloaded the 2 files from the mono/openlib page
and just followed those instructions:

So I did this:

wget http://www.ibiblio.org/pub/Linux/ALPHA/wine/development/Wine-20030318.tar.gz
wget http://www.openlinksw.com/mono/wine-shared-20030618.tar.gz
tar zxvf Wine-20030318.tar.gz
tar zxvf wine-shared-20030618.tar.gz
cd wine-20030318/
patch --strip=1 < ../wine-shared-20030519/wine/wine_diff
./configure --with-prefix=/usr/local
make wine-shared
make wine-shared-install

export SWF=1

And that did it.
I have a single screenshot at this time (only the most limited apps
worked, so it's a simple screenshot)

:)

I used WineLib with Mono 0.25 on Red Hat 9<BR>

<BR>
Then I downloaded the 2 files from the mono/openlib page<BR>
and just followed those instructions:<BR>
<BR>
So I did this:

./configure --with-prefix=/usr/local
